  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5af0971d-1260-405a-9547-2b317e21b2cd'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

La muerte y otras sorpresas es un libro que por muy sencillo que parezca, te introduce en un sin fin de historias que te atrapan y te hacen reflexionar sobre diferentes situaciones por las cuales pasan los seres humanos.   <span id="freeText12219708458977494551" style="display:none">Oh yes, Death and itâs other surprises. <br /><br />I love a good Mario Benedetti story. He is a keen observer of people and writes about their hard luck, ârise to the challengeâ lives and those love-hate relationships we all know. In short, he writes about life. <br /><br />So here is a little gem of a collection that lives up to itâs name, âDeath and other surprisesâ. The nineteen stories are very short, one is barely a page long and the longest, 22 pages. Most are five pages long but all have that âTwilight Zoneâ ghost story feel to them. Some are just plain creepy. This was something new for me in Benedettiâs oeuvre. <br /><br />My favourites were the longer ones at the back half. âAcaso irreparableâ is a guy waiting for his flight to take off, only to have it keep getting delayed to to mechanical issues. After three days, he sees a sign (oh itâs a great one). âEl cambiazoâ is a song played on the radio where the listeners get involved with the lyrics. The daughter of the colonel, in charge of torturing the prisoners, loves this song. Loves it to death. âCinco aÃ±os de vidaâ is not a charming love story between two strangers who get locked behind in a Paris Metro station at night. And the whole book kicks off with âLa muerteâ. A man having an affair gets diagnosed with not much to live for. Hmm. Just desserts?<br /><br />Plus he starts with an Antonio Machado quote, âif one lies more in the tale by lacking fantasy; the truth will invent itself too.â Perfect.<br /><br />If you have a love for great writing and a knack for ghost stories, who will enjoy this book.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12219708458977494551" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''

    }
  }

  }

Un conferencista extravÃ­a sus apuntes y el nerviosismo lo lleva a decir cosas impensadas. el tema de la charla es la relaciÃ³n entre la lluvia y la poesÃ­a amorosa. En el vÃ©rtigo de la improvisaciÃ³n, el protagonista habla de si mismo pero no abandona su propÃ³sito original; a su mente acuden los poetas que han cambiado el clima con sus versos. De manera fascinante se mezclan dos formas del discurso: la conferencia y la confesiÃ³n. Protagonizado por un bibliotecario, este monÃ³logo escrito por Juan Villoro es una honda y muchas veces irÃ³nica reflexiÃ³n sobre la vida de los libros y las emociones que despiertan. Una biblioteca es una colecciÃ³n de amores, repudios, sospechas y nostalgias, por lo que dicen sus volÃºmenes, pero tambiÃ©n por el modo en que han sido leÃ­dos.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/30195.Mario_Benedetti">About Mario Benedetti</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/30195.Mario_Benedetti"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1497449095p3/30195.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2389042048489078845">Mario Benedetti (full name: Mario Orlando Hamlet Hardy Brenno Benedetti Farugia) was a Uruguayan journalist, novelist, and poet. Despite publishing more than 80 books and being published in twenty languages he was not well known in the English-speaking world. He is considered one of Latin America's most important 20th-century writers.<br/><br/>Benedetti was a member of the 'Generation of 45', a Uruguayan in</span>
  <span id="freeText2389042048489078845" style="display:none">Mario Benedetti (full name: Mario Orlando Hamlet Hardy Brenno Benedetti Farugia) was a Uruguayan journalist, novelist, and poet. Despite publishing more than 80 books and being published in twenty languages he was not well known in the English-speaking world. He is considered one of Latin America's most important 20th-century writers.<br /><br />Benedetti was a member of the 'Generation of 45', a Uruguayan intellectual and literary movement and also wrote in the famous weekly Uruguayan newspaper Marcha from 1945 until it was forcibly closed by the military government in 1973, and was its literary director from 1954. From 1973 to 1985 he lived in exile, and returned to Uruguay in March 1983 following the restoration of democracy. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2389042048489078845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
